; ===============================================================================
; DIVERS-DIAL MASTER - 6502 Assembly Code
; ===============================================================================
; This appears to be a telecommunications/dial-up communication system
; for the 6502 processor, likely used for BBS (Bulletin Board System) or
; modem-based communications. The code includes:
; - Multi-channel communication handling (8 channels)
; - UART interface for serial communication  
; - Screen/display management
; - Command processing and parsing
; - Buffer management for input/output
; - System initialization and configuration
;
; COMMAND STRUCTURE (based on analysis):
; Commands appear to be in format: #<channel><command>
; Where channel is 0-9 and commands include:
; - M: Message/Mode command
; - O: Open/Online command  
; - A: Answer command
; - L: Line/Link command
; - F: Flip/Flag command
; - B: Break/Busy command
; - E: End/Exit command
; - X: eXchange command
; - C: Connect/Channel command
; - T: Terminal/Talk command
; ===============================================================================

; === MAIN INITIALIZATION ROUTINE ===
1800-  A2 FF     LDX #$FF          ; Initialize stack pointer to top of stack
1802-  9A        TXS                    ; Set stack pointer
1803-  20 9A 18  JSR $189A             ; Jump to initialization subroutine
1806-  A2 02     LDX #$02              ; Load X with 2 (loop counter)
1808-  BD FD 5E  LDA $5EFD,X          ; Load from data table at $5EFD+X
180B-  29 0F     AND #$0F              ; Mask to get lower 4 bits
180D-  09 30     ORA #$30              ; Convert to ASCII digit (add '0')
180F-  9D 3E 22  STA $223E,X          ; Store ASCII digit at $223E+X
1812-  CA        DEX                   ; Decrement X counter
1813-  10 F3     BPL $1808             ; Loop if X >= 0
1815-  AD 3D 60  LDA $603D             ; Load pointer low byte from $603D
1818-  85 00     STA $00               ; Store in zero page $00
181A-  AD 3E 60  LDA $603E             ; Load pointer high byte from $603E
181D-  85 01     STA $01               ; Store in zero page $01 (now $00/$01 is 16-bit pointer)
181F-  A0 00     LDY #$00              ; Initialize Y to 0
1821-  B1 00     LDA ($00),Y          ; Load byte from address pointed to by $00/$01
1823-  30 0C     BMI $1831             ; Branch if bit 7 set (negative)
1825-  C9 5E     CMP #$5E              ; Compare with '^' character
1827-  F0 08     BEQ $1831             ; Branch if equal to '^'
1829-  E6 00     INC $00               ; Increment low byte of pointer
182B-  D0 F4     BNE $1821             ; Branch if no overflow, continue loop
182D-  E6 01     INC $01               ; Increment high byte of pointer (handle overflow)
182F-  D0 F0     BNE $1821             ; Continue loop if high byte not zero
1831-  A5 00     LDA $00               ; Load found pointer low byte
1833-  8D 9B 60  STA $609B             ; Store pointer low byte at $609B
1836-  A5 01     LDA $01               ; Load found pointer high byte
1838-  8D 9C 60  STA $609C             ; Store pointer high byte at $609C
183B-  A0 00     LDY #$00              ; Initialize Y to 0
183D-  B9 00 1A  LDA $1A00,Y          ; Load byte from data table at $1A00+Y
1840-  F0 0E     BEQ $1850             ; Branch if zero (end of data)
1842-  99 00 E4  STA $E400,Y          ; Copy byte to $E400+Y
1845-  C8        INY                   ; Increment Y
1846-  D0 F5     BNE $183D             ; Continue loop if Y not zero
1848-  EE 3F 18  INC $183F             ; Increment source page (self-modifying code)
184B-  EE 44 18  INC $1844             ; Increment destination page (self-modifying code)
184E-  D0 ED     BNE $183D             ; Continue copy loop
1850-  4C B4 28  JMP $28B4             ; Jump to main program at $28B4

; === SUBROUTINE: Serial/Communication Handler ===
1853-  46 F2     LSR $F2               ; Shift right $F2 (communication flag)
1855-  24 D0     BIT $D0               ; Test bits in $D0
1857-  30 05     BMI $185E             ; Branch if bit 7 set
1859-  70 02     BVS $185D             ; Branch if overflow flag set
185B-  A0 8D     LDY #$8D              ; Load Y with carriage return code
185D-  60        RTS                   ; Return from subroutine
185E-  24 48     BIT $48               ; Test communication status
1860-  70 F9     BVS $185B             ; Branch if overflow set
1862-  AD 01 90  LDA $9001             ; Load from UART data register
1865-  F0 10     BEQ $1877             ; Branch if no data received
1867-  C9 7E     CMP #$7E              ; Compare with '~' character
1869-  F0 1C     BEQ $1887             ; Branch if '~' received
186B-  EE 63 18  INC $1863             ; Increment data counter (self-modifying)
186E-  D0 03     BNE $1873             ; Branch if no overflow
1870-  EE 64 18  INC $1864             ; Increment high byte counter
1873-  09 80     ORA #$80              ; Set bit 7 of received data
1875-  A8        TAY                   ; Transfer to Y register
1876-  60        RTS                   ; Return with received data in Y
1877-  A0 03     LDY #$03              ; Load Y with 3 (counter for 4 bytes)
1879-  B9 96 18  LDA $1896,Y          ; Load data from table at $1896+Y
187C-  99 D4 50  STA $50D4,Y          ; Store at $50D4+Y
187F-  88        DEY                   ; Decrement Y
1880-  D0 F7     BNE $1879             ; Loop until Y = 0
1882-  88        DEY                   ; Y = -1 ($FF)
1883-  8C FF FE  STY $FEFF             ; Store $FF at $FEFF (system flag)
1886-  60        RTS                   ; Return
1887-  A0 07     LDY #$07              ; Load Y with 7 (check 8 bytes)
1889-  B9 88 7F  LDA $7F88,Y          ; Load from status table at $7F88+Y
188C-  D0 07     BNE $1895             ; Branch if non-zero (channel active)
188E-  88        DEY                   ; Decrement Y
188F-  D0 F8     BNE $1889             ; Continue loop if Y != 0
1891-  A9 01     LDA #$01              ; All channels inactive, load 1
1893-  D0 D6     BNE $186B             ; Branch always (unconditional)
1895-  98        TYA                   ; Transfer Y to A (channel number)
1896-  60        RTS                   ; Return with channel number in A
1897-  AC F8 7F  LDY $7FF8             ; Load system status flag
; === SUBROUTINE: System Initialization at $189A ===
189A-  78        SEI                   ; Disable interrupts
189B-  A2 27     LDX #$27              ; Load X with $27 (screen size - 1)
189D-  A9 A0     LDA #$A0              ; Load A with $A0 (space character)
189F-  9D 00 04  STA $0400,X          ; Clear screen memory at $0400+X
18A2-  9D 80 04  STA $0480,X          ; Clear screen memory at $0480+X  
18A5-  CA        DEX                   ; Decrement X
18A6-  10 F7     BPL $189F             ; Loop while X >= 0 (clear screen)
18A8-  A9 0F     LDA #$0F              ; Load A with $0F
18AA-  C5 08     CMP $08               ; Compare with memory at $08
18AC-  85 08     STA $08               ; Store $0F at $08
18AE-  D0 05     BNE $18B5             ; Branch if $08 was not $0F
18B0-  A9 AE     LDA #$AE              ; Load A with $AE (different character)
18B2-  8D 88 04  STA $0488             ; Store at screen position $0488
18B5-  EE F4 03  INC $03F4             ; Increment system counter
18B8-  20 00 80  JSR $8000             ; Call subroutine at $8000
18BB-  AD 22 F8  LDA $F822             ; Load system configuration
18BE-  C9 60     CMP #$60              ; Compare with $60
18C0-  F0 05     BEQ $18C7             ; Branch if equal
18C2-  A9 4C     LDA #$4C              ; Load JMP opcode
18C4-  8D 79 39  STA $3979             ; Patch code at $3979 with JMP
18C7-  A2 07     LDX #$07              ; Load X with 7 (initialize 8 channels)
18C9-  20 08 60  JSR $6008             ; Call channel initialization
18CC-  CA        DEX                   ; Decrement X
18CD-  10 FA     BPL $18C9             ; Loop for all 8 channels
18CF-  A2 07     LDX #$07              ; Load X with 7 (8-byte copy)
18D1-  D0 08     BNE $18DB             ; Branch always (skip data table)

; Data table for memory initialization
18D3-  00        BRK                   ; $00
18D4-  80                              ; $80  
18D5-  00        BRK                   ; $00
18D6-  90 00     BCC $18D8             ; $90, $00
18D8-  A0 00     LDY #$00              ; $A0, $00
18DA-  B0                              ; $B0

18DB-  BD D3 18  LDA $18D3,X          ; Load from data table
18DE-  95 C0     STA $C0,X            ; Store in zero page $C0+X
18E0-  CA        DEX                   ; Decrement X
18E1-  10 F8     BPL $18DB             ; Loop until all 8 bytes copied
18E3-  A9 B1     LDA #$B1              ; Load A with $B1
18E5-  85 FD     STA $FD               ; Store at zero page $FD
18E7-  8D 80 04  STA $0480             ; Store at screen memory $0480
18EA-  A2 06     LDX #$06              ; Load X with 6
18EC-  86 E4     STX $E4               ; Store X at $E4
18EE-  A9 00     LDA #$00              ; Load A with 0
18F0-  85 E6     STA $E6               ; Clear $E6
18F2-  85 E3     STA $E3               ; Clear $E3
18F4-  85 E7     STA $E7               ; Clear $E7
18F6-  85 F7     STA $F7               ; Clear $F7
18F8-  85 F1     STA $F1               ; Clear $F1 (multiple variable initialization)
18FA-  AC 01 90  LDY $9001             ; Load Y from UART status register
18FD-  C0 0D     CPY #$0D              ; Compare Y with carriage return
18FF-  F0 03     BEQ $1904             ; Branch if equal (CR received)
1901-  8D 01 90  STA $9001             ; Store A to UART data register
1904-  81 C0     STA ($C0,X)          ; Store A using indirect addressing
1906-  CA        DEX                   ; Decrement X
1907-  CA        DEX                   ; Decrement X again (2-byte values)
1908-  10 FA     BPL $1904             ; Loop while X >= 0
190A-  A2 02     LDX #$02              ; Load X with 2 (3-byte loop)
190C-  A9 B0     LDA #$B0              ; Load A with $B0
190E-  9D 89 04  STA $0489,X          ; Store at screen memory $0489+X
1911-  CA        DEX                   ; Decrement X
1912-  10 FA     BPL $190E             ; Loop while X >= 0
1914-  A9 33     LDA #$33              ; Load A with '3' character
1916-  8D 00 04  STA $0400             ; Store at top-left of screen
1919-  A0 13     LDY #$13              ; Load Y with 19 (20-byte copy)
191B-  B9 B8 23  LDA $23B8,Y          ; Load from text table at $23B8+Y
191E-  09 80     ORA #$80              ; Set high bit (reverse video)
1920-  99 94 04  STA $0494,Y          ; Store at screen memory $0494+Y
1923-  88        DEY                   ; Decrement Y
1924-  10 F5     BPL $191B             ; Loop while Y >= 0 (copy title text)
1926-  A0 3F     LDY #$3F              ; Load Y with 63 (clear 64 bytes)
1928-  A9 00     LDA #$00              ; Load A with 0
192A-  99 00 01  STA $0100,Y          ; Clear stack page $0100+Y
192D-  88        DEY                   ; Decrement Y
192E-  10 FA     BPL $192A             ; Loop while Y >= 0 (clear stack page)
1930-  A9 D0     LDA #$D0              ; Load A with $D0 (starting page)
1932-  85 04     STA $04               ; Store as high byte pointer
1934-  A0 00     LDY #$00              ; Initialize Y to 0
1936-  84 03     STY $03               ; Store Y as low byte pointer ($03/$04 = pointer)
1938-  B9 DE 24  LDA $24DE,Y          ; Load from data table at $24DE+Y
193B-  91 03     STA ($03),Y          ; Store using indirect addressing
193D-  30 03     BMI $1942             ; Branch if high bit set (end marker)
193F-  C8        INY                   ; Increment Y
1940-  D0 F6     BNE $1938             ; Continue loop if Y != 0
1942-  E6 04     INC $04               ; Increment high byte of pointer
1944-  A5 04     LDA $04               ; Load current page
1946-  C9 F3     CMP #$F3              ; Compare with end page $F3
1948-  90 EA     BCC $1934             ; Continue if less than $F3 (copy more pages)
194A-  AD 0C 58  LDA $580C             ; Load configuration data
194D-  8D 51 60  STA $6051             ; Store at $6051
1950-  AD 0D 58  LDA $580D             ; Load more configuration data  
1953-  8D 52 60  STA $6052             ; Store at $6052
1956-  A9 34     LDA #$34              ; Load A with '4' character
1958-  8D 08 04  STA $0408             ; Store at screen position
195B-  60        RTS $1806             ; Return to caller (Note: unusual RTS with operand - likely disassembly error)
195C-  00        BRK
195D-  00        BRK
195E-  00        BRK
195F-  00        BRK

; === MAIN PROGRAM LOOP ===
28B4-  A9 40     LDA #$40              ; Load A with $40 (bit pattern)
28B6-  C5 90     CMP $90               ; Compare with system flag at $90
28B8-  F0 05     BEQ $28BF             ; Branch if equal (no change needed)
28BA-  85 90     STA $90               ; Update system flag
28BC-  8D 91 04  STA $0491             ; Update screen display
28BF-  20 D3 7F  JSR $7FD3             ; Call system update routine
28C2-  A5 F2     LDA $F2               ; Load main loop flag
28C4-  F0 03     BEQ $28C9             ; Branch if zero (first pass)
28C6-  4C 24 2A  JMP $2A24             ; Jump to continue main loop
28C9-  E6 F2     INC $F2               ; Set main loop flag (not first pass anymore)
28CB-  A5 A0     LDA $A0               ; Load input buffer status
28CD-  F0 4A     BEQ $2919             ; Branch if empty (no input to process)
28CF-  10 22     BPL $28F3             ; Branch if positive (normal input mode)
; Input processing when negative flag set
28D1-  A4 88     LDY $88               ; Load Y with input pointer
28D3-  C4 80     CPY $80               ; Compare with buffer end
28D5-  B0 2E     BCS $2905             ; Branch if at/past end (buffer full)
28D7-  B9 00 08  LDA $0800,Y          ; Load character from input buffer
28DA-  24 48     BIT $48               ; Test input flags  
28DC-  30 0F     BMI $28ED             ; Branch if bit 7 set
28DE-  50 05     BVC $28E5             ; Branch if overflow clear

28E5-  20 02 60  JSR $6002             ; Call output routine
